# Project: NBA Stats API v1.1 Beta Documentation

## NBA Stats API Documentation

Stats currently go back to the 2009-2010 season. More seasons are being added.

- New tests and Postman Visualizations added! - 07-24-2023.

View the Github project [here](https://github.com/nprasad2077/nbaStats).

## End-point: Player Season Stats by Name

_player name is specified in the url._

### Method: GET
>
>```
>https://nba-stats-db.herokuapp.com/api/playerdata/name/
>```
>
### Response: 200

## End-point: All Players by Season

_season is specified in the url._

### Method: GET
>
>```
>https://nba-stats-db.herokuapp.com/api/playerdata/season/2023
>```
>
### Response: 200

## End-point: Top Scorers by Season (Total Points)

## Return top players by total points in descending order

_Season is specified in the URL._

### Method: GET
>
>```
>https://nba-stats-db.herokuapp.com/api/playerdata/topscorers/total/season/2011/
>```
>
### 🔑 Authentication noauth

|Param|value|Type|
|---|---|---|

## End-point: Top Scorers in the Playoffs by Season (Total Points)

## End-point: Top Assists by Season (Total Assists)

## Return top 20 players by assists in descending order

_Season is specified in the URL._

### Method: GET
>
>```
>https://nba-stats-db.herokuapp.com/api/top_assists/totals/2011/
>```
>
### Response: 200


## End-point: Top Assists in the Playoffs by Season (Total Assists)

## Return top 20 players by assists (playoffs) in descending order

_Playoffs season is specified in the URL._

### Method: GET
>
>```
>https://nba-stats-db.herokuapp.com/api/top_assists/playoffs/2022/
>```

## End-point: Top Rebounders by Season (Total Rebounds)

## Return top players by total rebounds in descending order

_Season is specified in the URL._

### Method: GET
>
>```
>https://nba-stats-db.herokuapp.com/api/top_rebounds/totals/2023/
>```
>

## End-point: Player Shot Chart Data (Season & Playoffs)

## Return player shot chart data (season & playoffs)

### Current Players Available

- LeBron James
- James Harden
- Stephen Curry

_Player name and Season are specified in the request URL._

Shot chart is available [here](https://cdn.ssref.net/req/1/images/bbr/nbahalfcourt.png).

### Method: GET
>
>```
>https://nba-stats-db.herokuapp.com/api/shot_chart_data/Lebron James/2023/
>```
>
